commit dbb24cffffa316a5c7e939fa6cb44773b5abff88
Author: Ricardo Wurmus <rekado@elephly.net>
Date:   Fri Apr 5 22:42:26 2024 +0200

    Rename CMSIS directories in preparation for update.
    
    CMSIS DSP 1.6.0 splits headers into Core and DSP and drops the name
    "DSP_Lib" in favor of "DSP".  In order to generate a clearer diff when
    the actual upgrade happens, we already rename the directories here.

commit 853d2293628c2b9fdaf63daf007b1f32cb53de0f
Author: Ricardo Wurmus <rekado@elephly.net>
Date:   Sun Apr 7 00:10:05 2024 +0200

    Initialize LibUsb context before using it.
    
    getDeviceList can only be invoked after initializing LibUsb.  This may
    happen incidentally during other operations, but it is not guaranteed
    that LibUsb is initialized when USBPortSelectionDlg is populated.
    
    (Initializing LibUsb more than once is not a problem.)

commit 59bf67f3f763353115cc51cb540842cd9ed1b8f7
Merge: dfc412c6 26db22b1
Author: ksoloti <140304503+ksoloti@users.noreply.github.com>
Date:   Fri Apr 5 20:10:16 2024 +0800

    Merge pull request #1 from rekado/feature/fix-legacy-build-system
    
    legacy: Define SZ.

commit 26db22b13b5d792be5f3eed1c0e728bbefbce022
Author: Ricardo Wurmus <rekado@elephly.net>
Date:   Thu Apr 4 15:38:14 2024 +0200

    legacy: Define SZ.
    
    When `USE_VERBOSE_COMPILE` is `no`,
    `chibios/os/ports/GCC/ARMCMx/rules.mk` uses `$(SZ)` on the generated
    mounte and flasher binaries.  The `SZ` variable, however, is
    undefined and so `make` ends up attempting to execute the cross-built
    binaries on the host.
